                           PREMIUM PAYMENT PLAN AND DUE DATES
================================================================================
GL-BILL-001 policy form                                          Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0002,41670 / 007
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 107,692,General Aggregate: $2,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$5,546,CG 20 10 04 13

THE TOTAL ESTIMATED ANNUAL PREMIUM FOR POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS PAYABLE ACCORDING TO THE PAYMENT PLAN SELECTED AND OUTLINED IN YOUR BILLING STATEMENT.

Payments are due on the dates specified in your billing notices. Failure to remit payment by the due date may result in late fees or, ultimately, cancellation of the policy for nonpayment of premium.

We offer various payment options for your convenience. Please refer to your billing statement or contact our billing department for details on how to make payments and available installment plans.

It is the responsibility of the named insured to ensure that all premium payments are made on time. Nonpayment of premium is a serious matter that can lead to a lapse in coverage.

Any adjustments to the premium resulting from endorsements or audits will be reflected in subsequent billing statements and must be paid according to the revised schedule.

For questions regarding your billing statement or payment schedule, please contact Federal Casualty's billing department directly. Your producer, Maple Street Brokerage, can also assist with general inquiries.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC                                          GL-BILL-001

<table>
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="50%">

**THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.**

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

</td>
<td valign="top" width="50%">

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 16916 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

</td>
</tr>

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0006,61217 / 003
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Area 157,315,Medical Expense: $5,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$2,894,CG 24 26 12 19

THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC

THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES CERTAIN PROVISIONS OF THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE FORM, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, TO COMPLY WITH THE LAWS OF THE STATE OF VERMONT.

The cancellation provisions of this policy are amended as follows: If we cancel this policy for nonpayment of premium, we will provide at least 10 days' written notice. For all other reasons, we will provide at least 45 days' written notice.

The notice of cancellation or nonrenewal will be sent to the named insured at the mailing address shown in the declarations, 18 Harbor Park, Burlington, VT 05401. Proof of mailing will be sufficient proof of notice.

Any provision in the policy that conflicts with the minimum requirements of Vermont statutes concerning notice periods for cancellation or nonrenewal is hereby superseded by the terms of this endorsement.

This endorsement takes precedence over any conflicting language in the policy forms or other endorsements, to the extent required by Vermont law. All other terms and conditions of the policy remain unchanged.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

THIS POLICY IS ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, WITH A MAILING ADDRESS IN BURLINGTON, VT. CERTAIN PROVISIONS WITHIN THIS POLICY MAY BE MODIFIED OR SUPERSEDED BY THE LAWS AND REGULATIONS OF THE STATE OF VERMONT.

Where state law mandates specific policy language or conditions that differ from those presented in the standard forms, the state-mandated provisions will take precedence. This ensures compliance with local regulatory requirements.

Any amendatory endorsements specifically designed for Vermont will be attached to this policy and will detail the exact changes made to align with state statutes. These endorsements are part of your complete policy contract.

It is the insured's responsibility to be aware of and comply with all applicable state and local laws. This notice serves as a general reminder that state-specific rules can impact policy interpretation and application.

For detailed information regarding Vermont insurance regulations that may affect this Commercial General Liability policy, please consult with your legal counsel or the Vermont Department of Financial Regulation.

THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

THE PREMIUM FOR THIS COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS BASED ON INFORMATION PROVIDED AT THE INCEPTION OF THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS INFORMATION INCLUDES CLASSIFICATIONS, EXPOSURES, AND RATES.

We retain the right to conduct an audit of your books and records at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This audit is performed to determine the actual exposures and ensure the correct premium has been charged.

You agree to maintain accurate records of all information necessary for premium calculation, including but not limited to gross sales, payroll, and cost of work, corresponding to the exposure bases listed in the declarations.

If an audit reveals that the actual exposure differs from the estimated exposure, an adjustment to the premium will be made. If the adjusted premium is higher, you will owe us the additional amount. If it is lower, we will return the excess to you.

Failure to cooperate with an audit or to provide the necessary records may result in an estimated final premium calculation based on available information, which may be higher than the actual exposure.

The audit process is a standard practice in commercial insurance to ensure fairness and accuracy in premium determination for both the insured and the insurer.

THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

Definitions Applicable to General Liability Coverage
GL695378
04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

DEFINITIONS APPLICABLE TO GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE

CG 00 01 policy form
Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0017,10010 / 012
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 293,483,Damage to Premises Rented to You: $100,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$21,835,CG 20 37 04 13

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC

Limits of Insurance Provisions

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LIMITS OF INSURANCE PROVISIONS
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CG 00 01 policy form                                          Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0018,41670 / 001
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 312,398,Medical Expense: $5,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$3,498,CG 21 06 12 19

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Limits of Insurance Provisions                                          04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

===================================================================================================
                                  LIMITS OF INSURANCE PROVISIONS
===================================================================================================

CG 00 01 policy form                                                            Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0028,91560 / 003
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Payroll 450,422,Personal and Advertising Injury: $1,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$17,656,CG 24 04 01 24

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 91560 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC                                                                CG 00 01

                           PREMIUM AUDIT CONDITIONS

GL-AUD-001 policy form                                       Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0029,97047 / 012
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Area 457,845,Damage to Premises Rented to You: $100,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$17,947,CG 00 01 09 21

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

THE PREMIUM FOR THIS COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS BASED ON INFORMATION PROVIDED AT THE INCEPTION OF THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS INFORMATION INCLUDES CLASSIFICATIONS, EXPOSURES, AND RATES.

We retain the right to conduct an audit of your books and records at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This audit is performed to determine the actual exposures and ensure the correct premium has been charged.

You agree to maintain accurate records of all information necessary for premium calculation, including but not limited to gross sales, payroll, and cost of work, corresponding to the exposure bases listed in the declarations.

If an audit reveals that the actual exposure differs from the estimated exposure, an adjustment to the premium will be made. If the adjusted premium is higher, you will owe us the additional amount. If it is lower, we will return the excess to you.

Failure to cooperate with an audit or to provide the necessary records may result in an estimated final premium calculation based on available information, which may be higher than the actual exposure.

The audit process is a standard practice in commercial insurance to ensure fairness and accuracy in premium determination for both the insured and the insurer.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 97047 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Juniper Learning Center, LLC                                          GL-AUD-001

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

| **THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.** <br><br> In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses. <br><br> The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured. <br><br> No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage. <br><br> If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement. | We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. Where state law mandates specific policy language or conditions that differ from those presented in the standard forms, the state-mandated provisions will take precedence. This ensures compliance with local regulatory requirements.

Any amendatory endorsements specifically designed for Vermont will be attached to this policy and will detail the exact changes made to align with state statutes. These endorsements are part of your complete policy contract.

It is the insured's responsibility to be aware of and comply with all applicable state and local laws. This notice serves as a general reminder that state-specific rules can impact policy interpretation and application.

For detailed information regarding Vermont insurance regulations that may affect this Commercial General Liability policy, please consult with your legal counsel or the Vermont Department of Financial Regulation.

THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

WHO IS AN INSURED

THE NAMED INSURED, JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, AS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS, IS AN INSURED. THIS INCLUDES ANY INDIVIDUAL PARTNERS, MEMBERS, OR THEIR SPOUSES, BUT ONLY WITH RESPECT TO THE CONDUCT OF YOUR BUSINESS.

If the named insured is a limited liability company, its members are insureds, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. Its managers are also insureds, but only with respect to their duties as your managers.

Any executive officer or director of the named insured is an insured, but only with respect to their duties as an officer or director. Stockholders are also insureds, but only with respect to their liability as stockholders.

Any person or organization acting as your real estate manager is an insured. This applies only with respect to their duties as your real estate manager.

Any person or organization having temporary custody of your property if you die is an insured, but only with respect to liability arising out of the maintenance or use of that property.

Any newly acquired or formed organization, other than a partnership, joint venture, or limited liability company, over which you maintain ownership or majority interest, will be an insured for up to 90 days or until the end of the policy period, whichever is earlier.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 1 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, SPECIFICALLY REGARDING THE POLICY PERIOD AND CERTAIN COVERAGE ASPECTS.

The policy period, as stated in the declarations, is hereby clarified to commence on 04/01/2026 and conclude on 04/01/2027, at 12:01 A.M. Standard Time at the mailing address of the named insured.

Any reference to the policy period within the coverage forms or other endorsements shall be understood to mean this specified timeframe. No coverage is afforded for occurrences outside these dates unless explicitly stated otherwise by a separate endorsement.

This endorsement does not alter the limits of insurance or the classifications used for rating purposes. Its primary function is to ensure consistent application of the policy period across all components of the insurance contract.

All other terms, conditions, exclusions, and definitions of the policy remain in full force and effect, except as specifically amended by this endorsement.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

THE PREMIUM FOR THIS COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS BASED ON INFORMATION PROVIDED AT THE INCEPTION OF THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS INFORMATION INCLUDES CLASSIFICATIONS, EXPOSURES, AND RATES.

We retain the right to conduct an audit of your books and records at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This audit is performed to determine the actual exposures and ensure the correct premium has been charged.

You agree to maintain accurate records of all information necessary for premium calculation, including but not limited to gross sales, payroll, and cost of work, corresponding to the exposure bases listed in the declarations.

If an audit reveals that the actual exposure differs from the estimated exposure, an adjustment to the premium will be made. If the adjusted premium is higher, you will owe us the additional amount. If it is lower, we will return the excess to you.

Failure to cooperate with an audit or to provide the necessary records may result in an estimated final premium calculation based on available information, which may be higher than the actual exposure.

The audit process is a standard practice in commercial insurance to ensure fairness and accuracy in premium determination for both the insured and the insurer.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

**THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.**

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

The policy period, as stated in the declarations, is hereby clarified to commence on 04/01/2026 and conclude on 04/01/2027, at 12:01 A.M. Standard Time at the mailing address of the named insured.

Any reference to the policy period within the coverage forms or other endorsements shall be understood to mean this specified timeframe. No coverage is afforded for occurrences outside these dates unless explicitly stated otherwise by a separate endorsement.

This endorsement does not alter the limits of insurance or the classifications used for rating purposes. Its primary function is to ensure consistent application of the policy period across all components of the insurance contract.

All other terms, conditions, exclusions, and definitions of the policy remain in full force and effect, except as specifically amended by this endorsement.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

Definitions Applicable to General Liability Coverage

DEFINITIONS APPLICABLE TO GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE

CG 00 01 policy form
Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0032,47103 / 012
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
"Payroll 500,778",General Aggregate: $2,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$37,257,CG 21 06 04 13

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

GL-AUD-001 policy form                                              Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0037,97047 / 001
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Area 563,528,"Each Occurrence: $1,000,000"
PREMIUM,FORM
$6,311,CG 20 10 01 24

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

THE PREMIUM FOR THIS COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS BASED ON INFORMATION PROVIDED AT THE INCEPTION OF THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS INFORMATION INCLUDES CLASSIFICATIONS, EXPOSURES, AND RATES.

We retain the right to conduct an audit of your books and records at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This audit is performed to determine the actual exposures and ensure the correct premium has been charged.

You agree to maintain accurate records of all information necessary for premium calculation, including but not limited to gross sales, payroll, and cost of work, corresponding to the exposure bases listed in the declarations.

If an audit reveals that the actual exposure differs from the estimated exposure, an adjustment to the premium will be made. If the adjusted premium is higher, you will owe us the additional amount. If it is lower, we will return the excess to you.

Failure to cooperate with an audit or to provide the necessary records may result in an estimated final premium calculation based on available information, which may be higher than the actual exposure.

The audit process is a standard practice in commercial insurance to ensure fairness and accuracy in premium determination for both the insured and the insurer.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 97047 at Location 1 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THE PREMIUM FOR THIS COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS BASED ON INFORMATION PROVIDED AT THE INCEPTION OF THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS INFORMATION INCLUDES CLASSIFICATIONS, EXPOSURES, AND RATES.

We retain the right to conduct an audit of your books and records at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This audit is performed to determine the actual exposures and ensure the correct premium has been charged.

You agree to maintain accurate records of all information necessary for premium calculation, including but not limited to gross sales, payroll, and cost of work, corresponding to the exposure bases listed in the declarations.

If an audit reveals that the actual exposure differs from the estimated exposure, an adjustment to the premium will be made. If the adjusted premium is higher, you will owe us the additional amount. If it is lower, we will return the excess to you.

Failure to cooperate with an audit or to provide the necessary records may result in an estimated final premium calculation based on available information, which may be higher than the actual exposure.

The audit process is a standard practice in commercial insurance to ensure fairness and accuracy in premium determination for both the insured and the insurer.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.<br><br>The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit.                                WHO IS AN INSURED

CG 00 01 policy form                                         Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0010,41670 / 007
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 200,180,Personal and Advertising Injury: $1,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$14,893,CG 20 37 09 21

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

THE NAMED INSURED, JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, AS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS, IS AN INSURED. THIS INCLUDES ANY INDIVIDUAL PARTNERS, MEMBERS, OR THEIR SPOUSES, BUT ONLY WITH RESPECT TO THE CONDUCT OF YOUR BUSINESS.

If the named insured is a limited liability company, its members are insureds, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. Its managers are also insureds, but only with respect to their duties as your managers.

Any executive officer or director of the named insured is an insured, but only with respect to their duties as an officer or director. Stockholders are also insureds, but only with respect to their liability as stockholders.

Any person or organization acting as your real estate manager is an insured. This applies only with respect to their duties as your real estate manager.

Any person or organization having temporary custody of your property if you die is an insured, but only with respect to liability arising out of the maintenance or use of that property.

Any newly acquired or formed organization, other than a partnership, joint venture, or limited liability company, over which you maintain ownership or majority interest, will be an insured for up to 90 days or until the end of the policy period, whichever is earlier.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, SPECIFICALLY REGARDING THE POLICY PERIOD AND CERTAIN COVERAGE ASPECTS.**

The policy period, as stated in the declarations, is hereby clarified to commence on 04/01/2026 and conclude on 04/01/2027, at 12:01 A.M. Standard Time at the mailing address of the named insured.

Any reference to the policy period within the coverage forms or other endorsements shall be understood to mean this specified timeframe. No coverage is afforded for occurrences outside these dates unless explicitly stated otherwise by a separate endorsement.

This endorsement does not alter the limits of insurance or the classifications used for rating purposes. Its primary function is to ensure consistent application of the policy period across all components of the insurance contract.

All other terms, conditions, exclusions, and definitions of the policy remain in full force and effect, except as specifically amended by this endorsement.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 91560 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Definitions Applicable to General Liability Coverage

DEFINITIONS APPLICABLE TO GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE

CG 00 01 policy form
Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0017,10010 / 012
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 293,483,Damage to Premises Rented to You: $100,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$21,835,CG 20 37 04 13

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 97047 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

DEFINITIONS APPLICABLE TO GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE

CG 00 01 policy form                                                Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY

EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Area 373,406,Personal and Advertising Injury: $1,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$27,781,CG 00 01 01 24

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC                                             CG 00 01

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

The declarations page provides a summary of your coverage, including limits, deductibles, and the policy period. However, the full scope of your protection is defined by the coverage forms, conditions, and any attached endorsements.

Please pay close attention to all endorsements, as they may modify, restrict, or expand the coverage provided by the base policy forms. Endorsements are an integral part of your policy contract.

Should you have any questions about the terms, conditions, or exclusions of this policy, please contact your insurance producer, Maple Street Brokerage, at your earliest convenience.

Understanding your policy is vital for ensuring that your business operations are adequately protected. We recommend retaining all policy documents in a secure location for future reference.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 97047 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

Definitions Applicable to General Liability Coverage

DEFINITIONS APPLICABLE TO GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE

CG 00 01 policy form                                                           Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY

EXPOSURE,LIMIT
"Payroll 500,778",General Aggregate: $2,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$37,257,CG 21 06 04 13

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Where state law mandates specific policy language or conditions that differ from those presented in the standard forms, the state-mandated provisions will take precedence. This ensures compliance with local regulatory requirements.

Any amendatory endorsements specifically designed for Vermont will be attached to this policy and will detail the exact changes made to align with state statutes. These endorsements are part of your complete policy contract.

It is the insured's responsibility to be aware of and comply with all applicable state and local laws. This notice serves as a general reminder that state-specific rules can impact policy interpretation and application.

For detailed information regarding Vermont insurance regulations that may affect this Commercial General Liability policy, please consult with your legal counsel or the Vermont Department of Financial Regulation.

Limits of Insurance Provisions

LIMITS OF INSURANCE PROVISIONS

CG 00 01 policy form                                                           Policy No. GL695378

"ITEM","CLASS / TERRITORY"
"CGL-0038","61217 / 007"
"EXPOSURE","LIMIT"
"Area 591,086","General Aggregate: $2,000,000"
"PREMIUM","FORM"
"$30,440","CG 20 37 01 24"

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.
