THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 1 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

THE PREMIUM FOR THIS COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY POLICY, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, IS BASED ON INFORMATION PROVIDED AT THE INCEPTION OF THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS INFORMATION INCLUDES CLASSIFICATIONS, EXPOSURES, AND RATES.

We retain the right to conduct an audit of your books and records at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This audit is performed to determine the actual exposures and ensure the correct premium has been charged.

You agree to maintain accurate records of all information necessary for premium calculation, including but not limited to gross sales, payroll, and cost of work, corresponding to the exposure bases listed in the declarations.

If an audit reveals that the actual exposure differs from the estimated exposure, an adjustment to the premium will be made. If the adjusted premium is higher, you will owe us the additional amount. If it is lower, we will return the excess to you.

Failure to cooperate with an audit or to provide the necessary records may result in an estimated final premium calculation based on available information, which may be higher than the actual exposure.

The audit process is a standard practice in commercial insurance to ensure fairness and accuracy in premium determination for both the insured and the insurer.

**THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.**

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 91560 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

THE NAMED INSURED, JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, AS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS, IS AN INSURED. THIS INCLUDES ANY INDIVIDUAL PARTNERS, MEMBERS, OR THEIR SPOUSES, BUT ONLY WITH RESPECT TO THE CONDUCT OF YOUR BUSINESS.

If the named insured is a limited liability company, its members are insureds, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. Its managers are also insureds, but only with respect to their duties as your managers.

Any executive officer or director of the named insured is an insured, but only with respect to their duties as an officer or director. Stockholders are also insureds, but only with respect to their liability as stockholders.

Any person or organization acting as your real estate manager is an insured. This applies only with respect to their duties as your real estate manager.

Any person or organization having temporary custody of your property if you die is an insured, but only with respect to liability arising out of the maintenance or use of that property.

Any newly acquired or formed organization, other than a partnership, joint venture, or limited liability company, over which you maintain ownership or majority interest, will be an insured for up to 90 days or until the end of the policy period, whichever is earlier.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 97047 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Definitions Applicable to General Liability Coverage

DEFINITIONS APPLICABLE TO GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE

CG 00 01 policy form                                                           Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0007,18435 / 003
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 158,996,Each Occurrence: $1,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$8,188,CG 24 04 01 24

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 1 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC                                                                                                       CG 00 01

# LIMITS OF INSURANCE PROVISIONS

CG 00 01 policy form                                                           Policy No. GL695378

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0008,47103 / 003
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Payroll 171,494,General Aggregate: $2,000,000
PREMIUM,FORM
$8,831,CG 00 01 09 21

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

"BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.** | "Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada. |
| "Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured. | References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule. |
| An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy. | Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations. |
| "Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned. | If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date. |
| "Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization. | The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries. |

THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.

The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.

The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.

The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.

The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000.

Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

# Page 156

FEDERAL CASUALTY | COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY
Exclusion - Per- and Polyfluoroalkyl Substances (PFAS) 1

GL695378
04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

EXCLUSION - PER- AND POLYFLUOROALKYL SUBSTANCES (PFAS)

Endorsement No. GL-EN-001
Effective 01/20/2026

ITEM,CLASS / TERRITORY
CGL-0001,10010 / 003
EXPOSURE,LIMIT
Gross sales 87,042,"Each Occurrence: $1,000,000"
PREMIUM,FORM
$3,412,CG 00 01 01 24
ENDORSEMENT,EFFECTIVE DATE
GL-EN-001,01/20/2026
MATERIALITY,
No Material Change,

THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE FORM, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC. IT INTRODUCES AN EXCLUSION RELATED TO PER- AND POLYFLUOROALKYL SUBSTANCES (PFAS).

Notwithstanding any other provision of this policy, this insurance does not apply to bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury arising directly or indirectly out of the actual, alleged, or threatened presence, release, discharge, or dispersal of PFAS.

This exclusion applies regardless of the cause of the presence, release, discharge, or dispersal, and regardless of whether the PFAS are naturally occurring or man-made.

PFAS include, but are not limited to, perfluorooctanoic acid (PFOA), perfluorooctane sulfonic acid (PFOS), and any other related fluorinated organic compounds.

This exclusion encompasses any claim, demand, suit, or other action seeking damages, remediation costs, or any other relief related to PFAS.

All other terms, conditions, and exclusions of the policy remain in full force and effect. This endorsement is effective 01/20/2026, as indicated in the policy records.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 10010 at Location 1 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

This insurance does not apply to bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury arising directly or indirectly out of any actual or alleged access to or disclosure of confidential or personal information.

EXCLUSION - DATA PRIVACY VIOLATION

Endorsement No. GL-EN-023                                                         Effective 11/20/2026

ITEM,CGL-0023,CLASS / TERRITORY,18435 / 007
EXPOSURE,Gross sales 383,418,LIMIT,Damage to Premises Rented to You: $100,000
PREMIUM,$28,526,FORM,CG 20 10 01 24
ENDORSEMENT,GL-EN-023,EFFECTIVE DATE,11/20/2026
MATERIALITY,Administrative,,

THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE FORM, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC. IT ESTABLISHES AN EXCLUSION FOR CLAIMS RELATED TO DATA PRIVACY.

This insurance does not apply to bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury arising directly or indirectly out of any actual or alleged access to or disclosure of confidential or personal information.

This exclusion includes, but is not limited to, claims arising from the unauthorized collection, use, transmission, storage, or disposal of data, including electronic data, by any insured or by others for whom the insured is legally responsible.

Confidential or personal information includes, but is not limited to, private financial information, health information, or any other data that is protected by privacy laws or regulations.

This exclusion applies regardless of the means by which the access or disclosure occurred, whether through electronic or non-electronic methods, and regardless of intent.

All other terms, conditions, and exclusions of the policy remain in full force and effect. This endorsement is effective 03/20/2026, as indicated in the policy records.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE FORM, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC. IT ADDS CERTAIN PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS AS ADDITIONAL INSUREDS.

The person(s) or organization(s) shown in the Schedule of Additional Insureds are included as an insured, but only with respect to liability for bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury caused, in whole or in part, by your acts or omissions.

This coverage applies to liability arising out of your ongoing operations performed for that person or organization. It does not extend to independent acts or omissions of the additional insured.

The coverage afforded to the additional insured is limited to the scope of the written contract or agreement between you and that person or organization, if such a contract exists and requires you to provide such coverage.

The limits of insurance applicable to the additional insured will not exceed the lesser of the amount required by the contract or the limits shown in the declarations for Juniper Learning Center, LLC.

All other terms, conditions, exclusions, and definitions of the policy remain unchanged, except as specifically modified by this endorsement. This endorsement is effective as of the policy inception date unless otherwise specified.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Notwithstanding any other provision of this policy, this insurance does not apply to bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury arising directly or indirectly out of the actual, alleged, or threatened presence, release, discharge, or dispersal of PFAS.

# Exclusion - Data Privacy Violation 22

## EXCLUSION - DATA PRIVACY VIOLATION

Endorsement No. GL-EN-036                                                     Effective 12/20/2026

ITEM,CGL-0036,CLASS / TERRITORY,91560 / 003
EXPOSURE,Payroll 560,644,LIMIT,Medical Expense: $5,000
PREMIUM,$6,279,FORM,CG 00 01 09 21
ENDORSEMENT,GL-EN-036,EFFECTIVE DATE,12/20/2026
MATERIALITY,Administrative,,

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE FORM, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC. IT ESTABLISHES AN EXCLUSION FOR CLAIMS RELATED TO DATA PRIVACY.**

This insurance does not apply to bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury arising directly or indirectly out of any actual or alleged access to or disclosure of confidential or personal information.

This exclusion includes, but is not limited to, claims arising from the unauthorized collection, use, transmission, storage, or disposal of data, including electronic data, by any insured or by others for whom the insured is legally responsible.

Confidential or personal information includes, but is not limited to, private financial information, health information, or any other data that is protected by privacy laws or regulations.

This exclusion applies regardless of the means by which the access or disclosure occurred, whether through electronic or non-electronic methods, and regardless of intent.

All other terms, conditions, and exclusions of the policy remain in full force and effect. This endorsement is effective 03/20/2026, as indicated in the policy records.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 91560 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Products-Completed Operations Hazard Redefinition 23

================================================================================

                  PRODUCTS-COMPLETED OPERATIONS HAZARD REDEFINITION

Endorsement No. GL-EN-038                                                    Effective 02/20/2026

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
"ITEM","CGL-0038","CLASS / TERRITORY","61217 / 007"
"EXPOSURE","Area 591,086","LIMIT","General Aggregate: $2,000,000"
"PREMIUM","$30,440","FORM","CG 20 37 01 24"
"ENDORSEMENT","GL-EN-038","EFFECTIVE DATE","02/20/2026"
"MATERIALITY","No Material Change","",""
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE DEFINITION OF "PRODUCTS-COMPLETED OPERATIONS HAZARD" WITHIN THE COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY COVERAGE FORM, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, ISSUED TO JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC.

The definition of "products-completed operations hazard" is amended to clarify that it includes all bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of "your product" or "your work."

"Your work" is deemed completed at the earliest of the following times: when all of the work called for in your contract has been completed; when all of the work to be done at a site has been completed if your contract calls for work at more than one site; or when that part of the work has been put to its intended use by any person or organization other than another contractor or subcontractor working on the same project.

This redefinition is intended to provide greater clarity regarding the commencement of the completed operations phase for coverage purposes. It does not expand or restrict the overall scope of the products-completed operations aggregate limit.

The rates applied to the products-completed operations exposure, such as 0.071 or 0.160 as seen in the sample records, are based on this understanding of the hazard.

All other terms, conditions, exclusions, and definitions of the policy remain in full force and effect, except as specifically modified by this endorsement.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

The person(s) or organization(s) shown in the Schedule of Additional Insureds are included as an insured, but only with respect to liability for bodily injury, property damage, or personal and advertising injury caused, in whole or in part, by your acts or omissions.

This coverage applies to liability arising out of your ongoing operations performed for that person or organization. It does not extend to independent acts or omissions of the additional insured.

The coverage afforded to the additional insured is limited to the scope of the written contract or agreement between you and that person or organization, if such a contract exists and requires you to provide such coverage.

The limits of insurance applicable to the additional insured will not exceed the lesser of the amount required by the contract or the limits shown in the declarations for Juniper Learning Center, LLC.

All other terms, conditions, exclusions, and definitions of the policy remain unchanged, except as specifically modified by this endorsement. This endorsement is effective as of the policy inception date unless otherwise specified.

| **THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.**<br><br>The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence.<br><br>The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000.<br><br>The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000.<br><br>The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000. | Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy.<br><br>References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 91560 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.<br><br>Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.<br><br>If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.<br><br>The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.<br><br>Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.<br><br>A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued. |

THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

THROUGHOUT THIS POLICY, CERTAIN TERMS CARRY SPECIFIC MEANINGS. "BODILY INJURY" REFERS TO PHYSICAL HARM, ILLNESS, OR DISEASE SUSTAINED BY A PERSON, INCLUDING DEATH RESULTING FROM ANY OF THESE AT ANY TIME.

"Property damage" means physical injury to tangible property, including all resulting loss of use of that property. It also encompasses the loss of use of tangible property that has not been physically injured.

An "occurrence" is defined as an accident, including continuous or repeated exposure to substantially the same general harmful conditions. This definition is central to determining when coverage applies under this policy.

"Products-completed operations hazard" includes bodily injury and property damage occurring away from premises you own or rent and arising out of your product or work. Your work includes operations that have been completed or abandoned.

"Insured contract" means a contract or agreement pertaining to your business under which you assume the tort liability of another party to pay for bodily injury or property damage to a third person or organization.

"Coverage territory" refers to the United States of America (including its territories and possessions), Puerto Rico, and Canada.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

# Commercial General Liability Conditions

***

### COMMERCIAL GENERAL LIABILITY CONDITIONS

CG 00 01 policy form                                                              Policy No. GL695378

***

"ITEM","CLASS / TERRITORY"
"CGL-0004","91560 / 003"
"EXPOSURE","LIMIT"
"Payroll 127,051","Personal and Advertising Injury: $1,000,000"
"PREMIUM","FORM"
"$9,452","CG 21 06 09 21"

***

**THIS SECTION OUTLINES THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF BOTH THE INSURED AND THE INSURER UNDER THIS POLICY. COMPLIANCE WITH THESE CONDITIONS IS ESSENTIAL FOR THE PROPER ADMINISTRATION OF COVERAGE.**

In the event of an occurrence, offense, claim, or suit, the named insured, Juniper Learning Center, LLC, must provide prompt notice to us. This notice should include details regarding how, when, and where the incident took place, as well as the names and addresses of any injured persons and witnesses.

The insured must cooperate with us in the investigation, settlement, or defense of any claim or suit. This includes assisting in enforcing any right of contribution or indemnity against persons or organizations who may be liable to the insured.

No insured will, except at their own cost, voluntarily make a payment, assume any obligation, or incur any expense, other than for first aid, without our consent. Unauthorized actions may affect the availability of coverage.

If the named insured transfers their interest in this policy, our written consent is required. A transfer of rights and duties under this policy is not valid without our express agreement.

We retain the right to examine and audit your books and records related to this policy at any time during the policy period and for up to three years after its expiration. This is to ensure accurate premium determination.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 91560 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

***

Juniper Learning Center, LLC                                                                    CG 00 01

| **THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.**<br><br>We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.<br><br>The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.<br><br>This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.<br><br>The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of | claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.<br><br>References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 61217 at Location 6 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.<br><br>Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.<br><br>If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.<br><br>The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.<br><br>Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.<br><br>A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.<br><br>Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records. |

| | |
| :--- | :--- |
| **THE AMOUNTS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS FOR JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, POLICY NUMBER GL695378, REPRESENT THE MAXIMUM SUMS WE WILL DISBURSE, REGARDLESS OF THE NUMBER OF INSUREDS, CLAIMS MADE, OR PERSONS OR ORGANIZATIONS BRINGING SUIT.** <br><br> The "Each Occurrence Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all damages and medical expenses arising from any single occurrence. This limit is specified in the declarations, for example, $1,000,000 for Each Occurrence. <br><br> The "General Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage, and personal and advertising injury, other than those included in the products-completed operations aggregate. This limit is shown in the declarations, such as $2,000,000. <br><br> The "Products-Completed Operations Aggregate Limit" is the total maximum amount payable for all bodily injury and property damage arising from the products-completed operations hazard. This limit is also specified in the declarations, for example, $2,000,000. <br><br> The "Personal and Advertising Injury Limit" is the applicable ceiling for payment for the sum of all personal and advertising injury to any one person or organization. This limit is also detailed in the declarations, for instance, $1,000,000. | Defense costs are included within or outside these limits as specified in the declarations or applicable endorsements. It is important to review the declarations page for the specific limits that apply to this policy. <br><br> References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 47103 at Location 2 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule. <br><br> Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations. <br><br> If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date. <br><br> The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries. <br><br> Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy. <br><br> A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued. |

THE NAMED INSURED, JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, AS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS, IS AN INSURED. THIS INCLUDES ANY INDIVIDUAL PARTNERS, MEMBERS, OR THEIR SPOUSES, BUT ONLY WITH RESPECT TO THE CONDUCT OF YOUR BUSINESS.

If the named insured is a limited liability company, its members are insureds, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. Its managers are also insureds, but only with respect to their duties as your managers.

Any executive officer or director of the named insured is an insured, but only with respect to their duties as an officer or director. Stockholders are also insureds, but only with respect to their liability as stockholders.

Any person or organization acting as your real estate manager is an insured. This applies only with respect to their duties as your real estate manager.

Any person or organization having temporary custody of your property if you die is an insured, but only with respect to liability arising out of the maintenance or use of that property.

Any newly acquired or formed organization, other than a partnership, joint venture, or limited liability company, over which you maintain ownership or majority interest, will be an insured for up to 90 days or until the end of the policy period, whichever is earlier.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 41670 at Location 4 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

THIS COVERAGE PART OUTLINES THE PROTECTION PROVIDED FOR CERTAIN LIABILITIES ARISING FROM YOUR BUSINESS OPERATIONS. IT APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY AND PROPERTY DAMAGE OCCURRING DURING THE POLICY PERIOD, AS FURTHER DETAILED IN THE DECLARATIONS.

We will address sums that the insured becomes legally responsible to pay as damages due to covered bodily injury or property damage. This includes costs associated with the investigation and settlement of claims, or the defense of lawsuits, when such actions fall within the scope of this coverage.

The protection extends to incidents that take place within the coverage territory and during the policy period specified in the declarations. Specific exclusions and conditions, detailed elsewhere in this policy, may modify or remove certain aspects of this coverage.

This policy is issued to Juniper Learning Center, LLC, Policy Number GL695378, and provides the framework for your general liability protection. Please review all sections, including the declarations, schedules, and any attached endorsements, for a complete understanding of your coverage.

The coverage provided is subject to the limits of insurance shown in the declarations, which specify the maximum amounts payable for various types of claims. These limits are not cumulative and are subject to the aggregate limits described in this coverage part.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 16916 at Location 5 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of sales, payroll, area, contract cost, territory, products-completed operations, and other exposure records.

Juniper Learning Center, LLC

THE NAMED INSURED, JUNIPER LEARNING CENTER, LLC, AS SHOWN IN THE DECLARATIONS, IS AN INSURED. THIS INCLUDES ANY INDIVIDUAL PARTNERS, MEMBERS, OR THEIR SPOUSES, BUT ONLY WITH RESPECT TO THE CONDUCT OF YOUR BUSINESS.

If the named insured is a limited liability company, its members are insureds, but only with respect to the conduct of your business. Its managers are also insureds, but only with respect to their duties as your managers.

Any executive officer or director of the named insured is an insured, but only with respect to their duties as an officer or director. Stockholders are also insureds, but only with respect to their liability as stockholders.

Any person or organization acting as your real estate manager is an insured. This applies only with respect to their duties as your real estate manager.

Any person or organization having temporary custody of your property if you die is an insured, but only with respect to liability arising out of the maintenance or use of that property.

Any newly acquired or formed organization, other than a partnership, joint venture, or limited liability company, over which you maintain ownership or majority interest, will be an insured for up to 90 days or until the end of the policy period, whichever is earlier.

References to classification, territory, and exposure basis include class code 18435 at Location 3 only when that operation appears in the declarations or rating schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter limits, exclusions, additional-insured status, completed-operations treatment, or premium calculations.

If a form schedule and an endorsement detail page address the same operation, the endorsement detail controls from its effective date.

The insured should retain sales records, payroll records, contracts, leases, certificates, and location records used to support the exposure entries.

Coverage summaries on one page do not replace the limits schedule, exposure schedule, forms schedule, or exclusion endorsement attached to the policy.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend an exposure or additional-insured entry unless an endorsement is issued.
